\doxysection{rlgl.\+h}
\hypertarget{_classes_2lib_2rlgl_8h_source}{}\label{_classes_2lib_2rlgl_8h_source}\index{C:/Users/HP/Documents/GitHub/Minero-\/Game/Classes/lib/rlgl.h@{C:/Users/HP/Documents/GitHub/Minero-\/Game/Classes/lib/rlgl.h}}
\mbox{\hyperlink{_classes_2lib_2rlgl_8h}{Go to the documentation of this file.}}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{00001\ \textcolor{comment}{/**********************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00003\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ rlgl\ v4.5\ -\/\ A\ multi-\/OpenGL\ abstraction\ layer\ with\ an\ immediate-\/mode\ style\ API}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00005\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ An\ abstraction\ layer\ for\ multiple\ OpenGL\ versions\ (1.1,\ 2.1,\ 3.3\ Core,\ 4.3\ Core,\ ES\ 2.0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ that\ provides\ a\ pseudo-\/OpenGL\ 1.1\ immediate-\/mode\ style\ API\ (rlVertex,\ rlTranslate,\ rlRotate...)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ When\ choosing\ an\ OpenGL\ backend\ different\ than\ OpenGL\ 1.1,\ some\ internal\ buffer\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ initialized\ on\ rlglInit()\ to\ accumulate\ vertex\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ When\ an\ internal\ state\ change\ is\ required\ all\ the\ stored\ vertex\ data\ is\ renderer\ in\ batch,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ additionally,\ rlDrawRenderBatchActive()\ could\ be\ called\ to\ force\ flushing\ of\ the\ batch.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ Some\ additional\ resources\ are\ also\ loaded\ for\ convenience,\ here\ the\ complete\ list:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Default\ batch\ (RLGL.defaultBatch):\ RenderBatch\ system\ to\ accumulate\ vertex\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Default\ texture\ (RLGL.defaultTextureId):\ 1x1\ white\ pixel\ R8G8B8A8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Default\ shader\ (RLGL.State.defaultShaderId,\ RLGL.State.defaultShaderLocs)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ Internal\ buffer\ (and\ additional\ resources)\ must\ be\ manually\ unloaded\ calling\ rlglClose().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ CONFIGURATION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_11}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_21}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_33}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_43}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ GRAPHICS\_API\_OPENGL\_ES2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Use\ selected\ OpenGL\ graphics\ backend,\ should\ be\ supported\ by\ platform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Those\ preprocessor\ defines\ are\ only\ used\ on\ rlgl\ module,\ if\ OpenGL\ version\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ required\ by\ any\ other\ module,\ use\ rlGetVersion()\ to\ check\ it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RLGL\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Generates\ the\ implementation\ of\ the\ library\ into\ the\ included\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ If\ not\ defined,\ the\ library\ is\ in\ header\ only\ mode\ and\ can\ be\ included\ in\ other\ headers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ or\ source\ files\ without\ problems.\ But\ only\ ONE\ file\ should\ hold\ the\ implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RLGL\_RENDER\_TEXTURES\_HINT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Enable\ framebuffer\ objects\ (fbo)\ support\ (enabled\ by\ default)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Some\ GPUs\ could\ not\ support\ them\ despite\ the\ OpenGL\ version}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RLGL\_SHOW\_GL\_DETAILS\_INFO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Show\ OpenGL\ extensions\ and\ capabilities\ detailed\ logs\ on\ init}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RLGL\_ENABLE\_OPENGL\_DEBUG\_CONTEXT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Enable\ debug\ context\ (only\ available\ on\ OpenGL\ 4.3)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ rlgl\ capabilities\ could\ be\ customized\ just\ defining\ some\ internal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ values\ before\ library\ inclusion\ (default\ values\ listed):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_BATCH\_BUFFER\_ELEMENTS\ \ \ 8192\ \ \ \ //\ Default\ internal\ render\ batch\ elements\ limits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_BATCH\_BUFFERS\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 1\ \ \ \ //\ Default\ number\ of\ batch\ buffers\ (multi-\/buffering)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_BATCH\_DRAWCALLS\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 256\ \ \ \ //\ Default\ number\ of\ batch\ draw\ calls\ (by\ state\ changes:\ mode,\ texture)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_BATCH\_MAX\_TEXTURE\_UNITS\ \ \ \ 4\ \ \ \ //\ Maximum\ number\ of\ textures\ units\ that\ can\ be\ activated\ on\ batch\ drawing\ (SetShaderValueTexture())}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_MAX\_MATRIX\_STACK\_SIZE\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 32\ \ \ \ //\ Maximum\ size\ of\ internal\ Matrix\ stack}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_MAX\_SHADER\_LOCATIONS\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 32\ \ \ \ //\ Maximum\ number\ of\ shader\ locations\ supported}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_CULL\_DISTANCE\_NEAR\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 0.01\ \ \ \ //\ Default\ projection\ matrix\ near\ cull\ distance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_CULL\_DISTANCE\_FAR\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 1000.0\ \ \ \ //\ Default\ projection\ matrix\ far\ cull\ distance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ When\ loading\ a\ shader,\ the\ following\ vertex\ attribute\ and\ uniform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ location\ names\ are\ tried\ to\ be\ set\ automatically:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_POSITION\ \ \ \ \ "{}vertexPosition"{}\ \ \ \ //\ Bound\ by\ default\ to\ shader\ location:\ 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_TEXCOORD\ \ \ \ \ "{}vertexTexCoord"{}\ \ \ \ //\ Bound\ by\ default\ to\ shader\ location:\ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_NORMAL\ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}vertexNormal"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ //\ Bound\ by\ default\ to\ shader\ location:\ 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_COLOR\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}vertexColor"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ Bound\ by\ default\ to\ shader\ location:\ 3}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_ATTRIB\_NAME\_TANGENT\ \ \ \ \ \ "{}vertexTangent"{}\ \ \ \ \ //\ Bound\ by\ default\ to\ shader\ location:\ 4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_UNIFORM\_NAME\_MVP\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}mvp"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ model-\/view-\/projection\ matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_UNIFORM\_NAME\_VIEW\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}matView"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ view\ matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_UNIFORM\_NAME\_PROJECTION\ \ "{}matProjection"{}\ \ \ \ \ //\ projection\ matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_UNIFORM\_NAME\_MODEL\ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}matModel"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ model\ matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_UNIFORM\_NAME\_NORMAL\ \ \ \ \ \ "{}matNormal"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ normal\ matrix\ (transpose(inverse(matModelView))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_UNIFORM\_NAME\_COLOR\ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}colDiffuse"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ color\ diffuse\ (base\ tint\ color,\ multiplied\ by\ texture\ color)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_SAMPLER2D\_NAME\_TEXTURE0\ \ "{}texture0"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ texture0\ (texture\ slot\ active\ 0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_SAMPLER2D\_NAME\_TEXTURE1\ \ "{}texture1"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ texture1\ (texture\ slot\ active\ 1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RL\_DEFAULT\_SHADER\_SAMPLER2D\_NAME\_TEXTURE2\ \ "{}texture2"{}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ texture2\ (texture\ slot\ active\ 2)}}
